      /EJECT
      *****************************************************************
      * Entry parameters
     C           *ENTRY    PLIST
     C                     PARM           P0RTN   7
     C           P1SDSX    PARM           WP0001  1        Co-Packer Item
     C           P2HGCD    PARM           WP0002  70       Item Code
     C           P5C2CD    PARM           WP0003  70       Item Code Detai
      *****************************************************************
      * Initialize
     C                     EXSR ZZINIT
      *
      * Repeat forever
     C                     DO   *HIVAL
      * Display and process key screen
     C                     EXSR BADSKY
     C                     END
      *****************************************************************
      /EJECT
     CSR         BADSKY    BEGSR
      *================================================================
      * Display and process key screen
      *================================================================
      * Bypass first display of key screen is possible
     C           W0BYP     IFEQ *BLANK
     C                     MOVEL'Y'       W0BYP   1
     C                     END
      * Initialize key screen
     C                     EXSR MDIZ#K
      * Signal start of transaction
     C                     MOVEL'Y'       W0TRN   1
      *
     C           W0TRN     DOWEQ'Y'
     C           W0TRN     OREQ 'K'
      * Ensure transaction continues (if reset)
     C                     MOVEL'Y'       W0TRN   1
      * Set control to display first screen
     C                     Z-ADD1         W0SCR   30
      * Conduct screen conversation
     C           W0TRN     DOWEQ'Y'
      * Convert internal to external form
     C  N09                EXSR MNCV#K
      * Is bypass key screen still viable?
     C           W0BYP     IFEQ 'Y'
     C           #1HGCD    IFEQ *ZERO                      Item Code
      * One or more key fields is blank
     C           *IN30     OREQ '1'
      * HOME: Reset screen fields
     C                     MOVEL'N'       W0BYP
     C                     END
     C                     END
      * Bypass key screen
     C           W0BYP     IFEQ 'N'
      * Display key screen
     C                     EXSR BBEXFM
     C                     END
      * Cancel key screen bypass
     C                     MOVEL'N'       W0BYP
      * Process response to key screen
      * Cancel & exit program
     C   03                CAS            ZXEXPG
      * Switch between *ADD/*CHANGE modes
     C   09                CAS            BCCHMD
      * HOME: Reset screen fields
     C   30                CAS            BDHMKY
      * Process key screen input
     C                     CAS            BEPRKY
     C                     END
     C           W0TRN     DOWEQ'R'
     C                     MOVEL'Y'       W0TRN

      *================================================================
      * Convert fields into external form
      *================================================================
      * Convert Item Code to external.
      * CD7 Int/Ext
      * CASE: PAR.CD7 Int Numeric Key is not equal zero
     C           #1HGCD    IFNE 0                          *IF
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    WUEOCD           CD7 Ext Numeric
     C                     MOVEL#1HGCD    WUEOCD           CD7 Ext Numeric
      * CD7 Int/Ext EXCUSRSRC - *Field attribute types  * 
     C                     MOVEAWUEOCD    #L7              EDIT ARRAY
     C                     Z-ADD1         #E      30
     C                     MOVE *IN61     UUIN61  1
     C                     SETOF                     61
     C                     DO   7
     C           #L7,#E    IFEQ '0'                        ZERO VALUE
     C           *IN61     IFEQ '0'
     C                     MOVE ' '       #L7,#E
     C                     ADD  1         #E
     C                     END
     C                     ELSE
     C                     SETON                     61
     C                     END
     C                     END
     C                     MOVEA#L7       WUEOCD
     C                     MOVE UUIN61    *IN61
     C                     MOVELWUEOCD    V1HGCD           CD7 Ext Numeric
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: *OTHERWISE
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    V1HGCD           CD7 Ext Numeric
     C                     END                             *FI
      *================================================================
     CSR         MNEXIT    ENDSR
      /EJECT
     CSR         MOCV#D    BEGSR

      * Using LCL with the record status (to update to the Company Item)
      *    earlier function is saving the record status from the
      *    Item Default and compare here to know when to update
      *    the record status from the Item Default to the Company Item

      *    and the Company Item can also change the record status.
      *    only in the Company Item.

      * DB1 is the company item(before)
      * DB1 is being used on th fields that are maintained
      *     at the Edt Co/Item
      * LCL is from the unit weight

      * so change the db1 to PAR on these fields
      * 08/31/06 RMC chg par.print on schedule to db1.print on schedule

      * PK0318   Item tupe code change from/to FG/WP
      * CASE: DB1.Item Type Code NE PAR.Item Type Code
     C           WMN0CD    IFNE BYN0CD                     *IF
      * CASE:
      *  - c1ORc2
      *   |- c1    : DB1.Item Type Code is FG/WP
      *   |- c2    : PAR.Item Type Code is FG/WP
      *   '-
     C           WMN0CD    IFEQ 'FG'                       *IF
     C           WMN0CD    OREQ 'WP'
     C           BYN0CD    OREQ 'FG'                       *OR
     C           BYN0CD    OREQ 'WP'
      * Rtv/Chg for FG/WP typ IF
      * PK0318 - Item type code change from/to FG/WP
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    YL0057           Availability Gr
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    YL0058           Avail Group Cod
      * change from FG
      * CASE: PAR.Item Type Code is Finished Goods
     C           WMN0CD    IFEQ 'FG'                       *IF
     C                     MOVEL'ALL'     YL0057           Availability Gr
     C                     END                             *FI
      * change from WP
      * CASE: PAR.Item Type Code is Work in Process
     C           WMN0CD    IFEQ 'WP'                       *IF
     C                     MOVEL'WIP'     YL0057           Availability Gr
     C                     END                             *FI
      * change to   FG
      * CASE: PAR.Item Type Code USR is Finished Goods
     C           BYN0CD    IFEQ 'FG'                       *IF
     C                     MOVEL'ALL'     YL0058           Avail Group Cod
     C                     END                             *FI
      * change to   WP
      * CASE: PAR.Item Type Code USR is Work in Process
     C           BYN0CD    IFEQ 'WP'                       *IF
     C                     MOVEL'WIP'     YL0058           Avail Group Cod
     C                     END                             *FI
      * Rtv/Chg for FG/WP typ RT - Company Item/Avail Group  * 
     C                     EXSR TMRVGN
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI

      * Unit Weight Rules with Update on Item Default
      *================================================================
      * Set Allow Weight to Yes,
     C                     MOVEL'Y'       #DIFST           Allow Weight In
      * Test if there are currently any company items.
      * RTV Assign Co Flag     RT - Company Item  * 
      * Move input parameters to subroutine local variables.
     C                     Z-ADD#1HGCD    WL0144           Item Code
     C                     MOVELWUEDT1    WL0145    P      Company Assigne
     C                     EXSR SORVGN
      * Move subroutine local variables to output parameters.
     C                     MOVELWL0145    WUEDT1    P      Company Assigne
      * CASE: WRK.Company Assigned Usr NE WRK.BLANK
     C           WUEDT1    IFNE WUGSTX                     *IF
      * CASE: DTL.Item Type Code is FG/WP
     C           #1N0CD    IFEQ 'FG'                       *IF
     C           #1N0CD    OREQ 'WP'
      * If Catch Weight Sts = N (Std Weight every time)
      *                         (Unit weight will be maintained at itemlv
      * If Catch Weight Sts = Y (Unit weight will be maintained at complv
      * CASE: DTL.Catch Weight Status is no
     C           #1AVST    IFEQ 'N'                        *IF
      * Allow the user to change the Unit Wgt, and on update then
      * also update all the Company Item records for this item with
      * the unit weight from the Item default
     C                     MOVEL'Y'       #DIFST           Allow Weight In
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: DTL.Catch Weight Status is yes
     C           #1AVST    IFEQ 'Y'                        *IF
      * Once a company item has been created then the unit weight will
      * be maintained at the CoItem.  Item default unit's weight
      * will be displayed only.
     C                     MOVEL'N'       #DIFST           Allow Weight In
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: DTL.Item Type Code is Packaging and Supplies
     C           #1N0CD    IFEQ 'PS'                       *IF
      * Once a company item has been created then the unit weight will
      * be maintained at the CoItem.  Item default unit's weight
      * will be displayed only.
     C                     MOVEL'N'       #DIFST           Allow Weight In
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: DTL.Item Type Code is Raw Material
     C           #1N0CD    IFEQ 'RM'                       *IF
      * Allow the user to change the Unit Wgt, and on update then
      * also update all the Company Item records for this item with
      * the unit weight from the Item default
     C                     MOVEL'Y'       #DIFST           Allow Weight In
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
